-完全注解开发</a></span><span role="listitem" class="md-toc-item md-toc-h2" data-ref="n481"><a class="md-toc-inner" href="#spring整合log4j2">Spring整合log4j2</a></span><span role="listitem" class="md-toc-item href="#spring整合junit4和junit5">Spring整合JUnit4和JUnit5</a></span></p></div><h2 id='spring'><span>Spring</span></h2><p><strong><span>Spring的概述</span></strong></p><blockquote><ol start='' ><li><span>针对bean的生命周期管理的轻量级容器，开源的JavaEE的框架</span></li><li><strong><span>目的：</span></strong><span>解决企业应用开发的复杂性，使开发更加简洁</span></li><li><strong><span>Spring的组成部分（核心）:</span></strong></li></ol><blockquote><p><span>IOC:控制反转，把创建对象交给Spring进行管理，和javaweb的那个配置bean xml相似</span></p><p><span>AOP:面向切面，不修改源代码的情况下进行功能的添加</span></p></blockquote><ol start='4' ><li><strong><span>特点:</span></strong></li></ol><blockquote><p><span>方便解耦，简化开发，降低耦合度</span></p><p><span>内置junit，方便测试</span></p><p><span>可以整合其他框架，mybatis，hibernate</span></p><p><span>方便进行事务的操作，降低了API开发的难度，对JDBC进行了封装</span></p><p><span>Spring的源码设计巧妙，对源码的学习可以对开发有很好的帮助</span></p></blockquote></blockquote><h2 id='spring5的下载'><span>Spring5的下载</span></h2><blockquote><p>🚀<span>下载地址:</span><a href='https://repo.spring.io/release/org/springframework/spring/' target='_blank' class='url'>https://repo.spring.io/release/org/springframework/spring/</a></p><p><span>下载最新的稳定版 5.2.6</span></p><p><span>commons-logging -1.1.1.jar 的下载地址:</span></p><p>🚀<a href='https://repo1.maven.org/maven2/commons-logging/commons-logging/1.1.1/' target='_blank' class='url'>https://repo1.maven.org/maven2/commons-logging/commons-logging/1.1.1/</a></p><p><span>使用Spring:</span></p><blockquote><p><span>基础首先导入四个核心的jar包，和一个logging包</span></p><p><span>spring-beans-5.2.6.RELEASE.jar</span></p><p><span>spring-core-5.2.6.RELEASE.jar</span></p><p><span>spring-context-5.2.6.RELEASE.jar</span></p><p><span>spring-expression-5.2.6.RELEASE.jar</span></p><p><span>commons-logging-1.1.1.jar</span></p></blockquote></blockquote><p><strong><u><span>使用配置文件的方式</span></u></strong></p><pre height: 0px; width: 1px; border-bottom: 0px solid transparent; top: 230px;"></div><div class="CodeMirror-gutters" style="display: none; height: 230px;"></div></div></div></pre><h2 id='ioc的原理和概念'><span>IOC的原理和概念</span></h2><p>➡️<strong><span>本节学习内容:</span></strong></p><p><span>	</span><span>&gt; </span><strong><span>IOC容器</span></strong></p><p><span>			</span><span>&gt;IOC的底层原理</span></p><p><span>			</span><span>&gt; IOC接口（beanFactory）</span></p><p><span>			</span><span>&gt; IOC操作bean管理(基于xml)</span></p><p><span>			</span><span>&gt; IOC操作bean管理(基于注解)</span></p><ol start='' ><li><strong><span>什么是IOC</span></strong></li></ol><blockquote><p><span>控制反转，把对象的创建和对象之间的调用交给Spring进行管理</span></p><p><span>使用IOC的目的，降低耦合度</span></p></blockquote><ol start='2' ><li><strong><span>IOC的底层原理是</span></strong></li></ol><blockquote><p><span>xml解析，反射，工厂模式</span></p><p><span>所谓工厂模式就是使用一个bean工厂的类里面放所有的对象，需要的话直接getBean(需要的类)</span></p></blockquote><ol start='3' ><li><p><strong><span>IOC的实现过程</span></strong></p><pre class="md-fences md-end-block ty-contain-cm modeLoaded" spellcheck="false" lang="java"><div class="CodeMirror cm-s-inner cm-s-null-scroll CodeMirror-wrap" lang="java"><div style="overflow: hidden; position: relative; width: 3px; height: 0px; top: 10.8px; left: 4px;"><textarea autocorrect="off" autocapitalize="off" spellcheck="false" tabindex="0" style="position: absolute; bottom: -1em; padding: 0px; width: 1000px; height: 1em; outline: none;"></textarea></div><div class="CodeMirror-scrollbar-filler" cm-not-content="true"></div><div class="CodeMirror-gutter-filler" cm-not-content="true"></div><div class="CodeMirror-scroll" tabindex="-1"><div class="CodeMirror-sizer" style="margin-left: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; border-right-width: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px;"><div style="position: relative; top: 0px;"><div class="CodeMirror-lines" role="presentation"><div role="presentation" style="position: relative; outline: none;"><div class="CodeMirror-measure"><pre><span>xxxxxxxxxx</span></pre></div><div class="CodeMirror-measure"></div><div style="position: relative; z-index: 1;"></div><div class="CodeMirror-code" role="presentation" style=""><div class="CodeMirror-activeline" style="position: relative;"><div class="CodeMirror-activeline-background CodeMirror-linebackground"></div><div class="CodeMirror-gutter-background CodeMirror-activeline-gutter" style="left: 0px; width: 0px;"></div><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"><span class="cm-variable">首先在配置文件中配置创建的对象</span></span></pre></div><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"> &nbsp; &nbsp;<span class="cm-operator">&lt;</span><span class="cm-variable">bean</span> <span class="cm-variable">id</span><span class="cm-operator">=</span><span class="cm-string">"userDAO"</span> <span class="cm-keyword">class</span><span class="cm-operator">=</span><span class="cm-string">"com.wjh.dao.impl.UserDAO"</span><span class="cm-operator">&gt;&lt;/</span><span class="cm-variable">bean</span><span class="cm-operator">&gt;</span></span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"><span cm-text="" cm-zwsp="">
</span></span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"><span class="cm-variable">然后创建一个工厂类</span></span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"> &nbsp; &nbsp;<span class="cm-keyword">class</span> <span class="cm-def">UserFactory</span>(){</span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"> &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;<span class="cm-keyword">public</span> <span class="cm-keyword">static</span> <span class="cm-variable">UserDAO</span> <span class="cm-variable">getUserDAO</span>(){</span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"> &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;<span class="cm-variable-3">String</span> <span class="cm-variable">valueClass</span> <span class="cm-operator">=</span> <span class="cm-variable">classs属性的内容</span>; <span class="cm-variable">使用xml解析技术</span></span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"> &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;<span class="cm-variable">Class</span> <span class="cm-variable">clazz</span> <span class="cm-operator">=</span> <span class="cm-variable">Class</span>.<span class="cm-variable">forName</span>(<span class="cm-variable">valueClass</span>); <span class="cm-variable">通过反射获取到这个大Class对象</span></span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"> &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;<span class="cm-keyword">return</span> (<span class="cm-variable">UserDAO</span>)<span class="cm-variable">clazz</span>.<span class="cm-variable">newInstance</span>(); &nbsp; &nbsp;</span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"> &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;  }</span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"> &nbsp;  }</span></pre></div></div></div></div></div><div style="position: absolute; height: 0px; width: 1px; border-bottom: 0px solid transparent; top: 282px;"></div><div class="CodeMirror-gutters" style="display: none; height: 282px;"></div></div></div></pre><ol start='4' ><li><p><strong><span>IOC的接口</span></strong></p><blockquote><p><span>IOC是基于IOC容器完成，IOC容器底层是对象工厂</span></p><p><span>Spring提供实现IOC的两种方式: IOC接口：</span></p><blockquote><p><span>BeanFactory:IOC容器的基本实现，是spring内部使用的接口</span></p><blockquote><p><span>加载配置文件的时候不会创建类的对象，在获取对象的时候才会创建</span></p></blockquote><p><span>ApplicationContext:是BeanFactory的一个子接口，一般开发人员使用这个</span></p><blockquote><p><span>加载配置文件的时候创建对象，好处是用户体验比较强，在服务器启动的时候就把对象创建了</span></p></blockquote></blockquote></blockquote></li></ol></li></ol><h2 id='ioc的bean管理基于xml）'><span>IOC的bean管理（基于XML）</span></h2><h3 id='无参的构造方法set方式注入属性'><span>无参的构造方法(set方式注入属性)</span></h3><ol start='' ><li><p><strong><span>对象的创建（xml）</span></strong></p><p><span>在bean标签中两个重要的属性 </span></p><blockquote><p><span>id:唯一表示，获取这个class的标识</span></p><p><span>class: 类全路径</span></p></blockquote><p><bean id="user" class="com.wjh.learnspring.User"/><span>（默认调用类的无参构造方法）</span></p></li><li><p><strong><span>属性的注入（xml）</span></strong></p><p><span>DI:依赖注入，即把注入属性，先创建对象，再注入属性</span></p><p><span>在bean标签中的子标签property</span></p><blockquote><p><span>name:类中属性的名字</span></p><p><span>ref:自定义类的bean名称</span></p><p><span>value: 注入的值</span></p></blockquote><p><bean id="user" class="com.wjh.learnspring.User">
<span>        </span><property name="userName" value="通过xml注入属性"/>
</bean></p></li></ol><h3 id='有参数的构造方法的创建和注入'><span>有参数的构造方法的创建和注入</span></h3><ol start='' ><li><p><strong><span>对象的创建</span></strong></p><pre class="md-fences md-end-block ty-contain-cm modeLoaded" spellcheck="false" lang="xml"><div class="CodeMirror cm-s-inner cm-s-null-scroll CodeMirror-wrap" lang="xml"><div style="overflow: hidden; height: 898px;"></div></div></div></pre><h3 id='bean的作用域'><span>bean的作用域</span></h3><ol start='' ><li><p><span>在Spring中，可以设置bean实例是单例的还是多实例的</span></p></li><li><p><span>在bean标签中设置，scope属性，有两个常用的值</span></p><blockquote><p><strong><span>singleton:</span></strong><span>单实例对象 默认是单实例</span></p><p><strong><span>prototype:</span></strong><span>多实例对象</span></p></blockquote><p><strong><span>singleton 和 prototype的区别？</span></strong></p><ol start='' ><li><p><span>一个是单实例一个是多实例</span></p></li><li><p><span>singleton在加载配置文件的时候，解析xml的时候就已经创建好实例对象了</span></p><p><span>prototype在getBean()的时候才会创建实例对象</span></p></li></ol></li></ol><p><span>单例是创建的对象是一个地址一样</span></p><p><span>com.wjh.learnspring.User@515c6049</span>
<span>com.wjh.learnspring.User@515c6049</span></p><p><span>多实例是不一样的地址</span></p><p><span>com.wjh.learnspring.User@48f2bd5b</span>
<span>com.wjh.learnspring.User@7b2bbc3</span></p><h3 id='bean的生命周期'><span>bean的生命周期</span></h3><p><strong><span>生命周期</span></strong></p><p><span>从对象的创建到销毁的过程</span></p><p><strong><span>bean的生命周期</span></strong></p><ul><li><span>通过调用无参的构造方法创建bean实例</span></li><li><span>调用set方法为bean的属性设置值和对其他bean的引用</span></li><li><span>调用bean的初始化方法（需要配置初始化方法）</span></li><li><span>此时bean就可以使用了</span></li><li><span>当容器关闭的时候，调用bean的销毁方法（需要配置销毁的方法）</span></li></ul><pre class="md-fences md-end-block ty-contain-cm modeLoaded" spellcheck="false" lang="java" style="break-inside: unset;"><div class="CodeMirror cm-s-inner cm-s-null-scroll CodeMirror-wrap" lang="java"><div style="overflow: hidden; width: 1000px; height: 1em; outline: none;"></textarea></div><div class="CodeMirror-scrollbar-filler" cm-not-content="true"></div><div class="CodeMirror-gutter-filler" cm-not-content="true"></div><div class="CodeMirror-scroll" tabindex="-1"><div class="CodeMirror-sizer" style="margin-left: 0px; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;<span class="cm-tag cm-bracket">&lt;</span><span class="cm-tag">property</span> <span class="cm-attribute">name</span>=<span class="cm-string">"password"</span> <span class="cm-attribute">value</span>=<span class="cm-string">"${jdbc.password}"</span><span class="cm-tag cm-bracket">/&gt;</span></span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"> &nbsp; &nbsp;<span class="cm-tag cm-bracket">&lt;/</span><span class="cm-tag">bean</span><span class="cm-tag cm-bracket">&gt;</span></span></pre></div></div></div></div></div><div style="position: absolute; height: 0px; width: 1px; border-bottom: 0px solid transparent; top: 640px;"></div><div class="CodeMirror-gutters" style="display: none; height: 640px;"></div></div></div></pre><h2 id='ioc的bean管理基于注解）'><span>IOC的bean管理（基于注解）</span></h2><h3 id='使用注解创建对象'><span>使用注解创建对象</span></h3><p><strong><span>什么是注解?</span></strong></p><ul><li><span>注解是特殊代码标记，格式是@注解名称(属性=值，属性=值)</span></li><li><span>注解是可以使用在类上，属性上，方法上</span></li><li><span>使用注解可以简化xml配置</span></li></ul><p><strong><span>Spring中创建对象提供四个注解</span></strong></p><ul><li><span>@Component</span></li><li><span>@Service //一般在service层使用</span></li><li><span>@Controller //一般在controller层</span></li><li><span>@Reposity //一般在dao层使用</span></li></ul><p><strong><span>上面四个注解功能是一样的，都可以来创建bena实例</span></strong></p><p><span>引入注解步骤是:</span></p><p><strong><span>第一步 导入依赖</span></strong></p><p><span>spring-aop-5.2.6.RELEASE.jar</span></p><p><strong><span>第二步 扫描组件</span></strong></p><p><span>在xml中引入命名空间</span></p><pre class="md-fences md-end-block ty-contain-cm modeLoaded" spellcheck="false" lang="xml"><div class="CodeMirror cm-s-inner cm-s-null-scroll CodeMirror-wrap" lang="xml"><div style="overflow: hidden; position: relative; width: 3px; height: 0px; top: 10.8px; left: 4px;"><textarea autocorrect="off" autocapitalize="off" spellcheck="false" tabindex="0" style="position: absolute; bottom: -1em; padding: 0px; width: 1000px; height: 1em; outline: none;"></textarea></div><div class="CodeMirror-scrollbar-filler" cm-not-content="true"></div><div class="CodeMirror-gutter-filler" cm-not-content="true"></div><div class="CodeMirror-scroll" tabindex="-1"><div class="CodeMirror-sizer" style="margin-left: 0px; &nbsp;<span class="cm-comment">&lt;!--开启组件扫描</span></span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"> &nbsp; &nbsp;<span class="cm-comment">1. 如果是多个包，可以使用逗号隔开  com.wjh.learnspring2.dao,com.wjh.learnspring2.service</span></span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"> &nbsp; &nbsp;<span class="cm-comment">2 .也可以直接是上一级包名 com.wjh</span></span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"><span class="cm-tab" role="presentation" cm-text="	">    </span><span class="cm-comment">--&gt;</span></span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"><span class="cm-tag cm-bracket">&lt;</span><span class="cm-tag">context:component-scan</span> <span class="cm-attribute">base-package</span>=<span class="cm-string">"com.wjh"</span><span class="cm-tag cm-bracket">/&gt;</span></span></pre></div></div></div></div></div><div style="position: absolute; width: 0px;"></div><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"><span class="cm-comment">&lt;!--use-default-filters="false" 表示不适用默认的filters  自己配置filters</span></span></pre></div><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"> &nbsp; &nbsp;<span class="cm-comment">&lt;context:include-filter&gt; 表示扫描使用Controller的注解</span></span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"> &nbsp; &nbsp;<span class="cm-comment">&lt;context:exclude-filter&gt; 表示排除使用Controller的注解</span></span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"><span class="cm-comment">--&gt;</span></span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"><span class="cm-tag cm-bracket">&lt;</span><span class="cm-tag">context:component-scan</span> <span class="cm-attribute">base-package</span>=<span class="cm-string">"com.wjh"</span> <span class="cm-attribute">use-default-filters</span>=<span class="cm-string">"false"</span><span class="cm-tag cm-bracket">&gt;</span></span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"> &nbsp; &nbsp;<span class="cm-tag cm-bracket">&lt;</span><span class="cm-tag">context:include-filter</span> <span class="cm-attribute">type</span>=<span class="cm-string">"annotation"</span> <span class="cm-attribute">expression</span>=<span class="cm-string">"org.springframework.stereotype.Controller"</span><span class="cm-tag cm-bracket">/&gt;</span></span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"><span class="cm-tag cm-bracket">&lt;/</span><span class="cm-tag">context:component-scan</span><span class="cm-tag cm-bracket">&gt;</span></span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"><span cm-text="" cm-zwsp="">
</span></span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"><span class="cm-tag cm-bracket">&lt;</span><span class="cm-tag">context:component-scan</span> <span class="cm-attribute">base-package</span>=<span class="cm-string">"com.wjh"</span><span class="cm-tag cm-bracket">&gt;</span></span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"> &nbsp; &nbsp;<span class="cm-tag cm-bracket">&lt;</span><span class="cm-tag">context:exclude-filter</span> <span class="cm-attribute">type</span>=<span class="cm-string">"annotation"</span> <span class="cm-attribute">expression</span>=<span class="cm-string">"org.springframework.stereotype.Controller"</span><span class="cm-tag cm-bracket">/&gt;</span></span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"><span class="cm-tag cm-bracket">&lt;/</span><span class="cm-tag">context:component-scan</span><span class="cm-tag cm-bracket">&gt;</span></span></pre></div></div></div></div></div><div style="position: absolute; height: 0px; width: 1px; border-bottom: 0px solid transparent; top: 282px;"></div><div class="CodeMirror-gutters" style="display: none; height: 282px;"></div></div></div></pre><h3 id='属性注入'><span>属性注入</span></h3><p><span>属性注入有三个注解</span></p><ul><li><span>@Autowired  根据类型进行注入</span></li><li><span>@Qualifier 根据名称进行注入</span></li><li><span>@Resource  既可以根据类型，也可以根据名称</span></li><li><span>@value 表示注入基本属性类型，以上三个是自定义的类型注入</span></li></ul><pre class="md-fences md-end-block ty-contain-cm modeLoaded" spellcheck="false" lang="java" style="break-inside: unset;"><div class="CodeMirror cm-s-inner cm-s-null-scroll CodeMirror-wrap" lang="java"><div style="overflow: hidden; position: relative; width: 3px; height: 0px; top: 10.8px; left: 4px;"><textarea autocorrect="off" autocapitalize="off" spellcheck="false" tabindex="0" style="position: absolute; bottom: -1em; padding: 0px; width: 1000px; height: 1em; outline: none;"></textarea></div><div class="CodeMirror-scrollbar-filler" cm-not-content="true"></div><div class="CodeMirror-gutter-filler" cm-not-content="true"></div><div class="CodeMirror-scroll" tabindex="-1"><div class="CodeMirror-sizer" style="margin-left: 0px; outline: none;"><div class="CodeMirror-measure"><pre><span>xxxxxxxxxx</span></pre></div><div class="CodeMirror-measure"></div><div style="position: relative; z-index: 1;"></div><div class="CodeMirror-code" role="presentation" style=""><div class="CodeMirror-activeline" style="position: relative;"><div class="CodeMirror-activeline-background CodeMirror-linebackground"></div><div class="CodeMirror-gutter-background CodeMirror-activeline-gutter" style="left: 0px; width: 0px;"></div><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"><span class="cm-comment">//@Autowired  @Qualifier 的使用</span></span></pre></div><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"><span class="cm-meta">@Service</span></span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"><span class="cm-keyword">public</span> <span class="cm-keyword">class</span> <span class="cm-def">UserService</span> {</span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"><span cm-text="" cm-zwsp="">
</span></span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"> &nbsp; &nbsp;<span class="cm-comment">//表示根据属性类型自动注入，不用写set方法，里面已经封装了</span></span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"> &nbsp; &nbsp;<span class="cm-comment">//使用Qualifier 必须要和Autowired配和使用，目的是，如果UserDAO有多个实现类的话 指定名称就可以指定某一个实现类</span></span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"> &nbsp; &nbsp;<span class="cm-meta">@Autowired</span></span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"> &nbsp; &nbsp;<span class="cm-meta">@Qualifier</span>(<span class="cm-variable">value</span> <span class="cm-operator">=</span> <span class="cm-string">"userDAOImpl2"</span>)</span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"> &nbsp; &nbsp;<span class="cm-keyword">public</span> <span class="cm-variable">UserDAO</span> <span class="cm-variable">userDAO</span>;</span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"><span cm-text="" cm-zwsp="">
</span></span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"> &nbsp; &nbsp;<span class="cm-keyword">public</span> <span class="cm-variable-3">void</span> <span class="cm-variable">add</span>() {</span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"> &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;<span class="cm-variable">System</span>.<span class="cm-variable">out</span>.<span class="cm-variable">println</span>(<span class="cm-string">"Service add......."</span>);</span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"> &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;<span class="cm-variable">userDAO</span>.<span class="cm-variable">add</span>();</span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"> &nbsp;  }</span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;">}</span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"><span cm-text="" cm-zwsp="">
</span></span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"><span class="cm-comment">//@Resource 注解的使用 &nbsp; 属于 javax.annotation.Resource;  Spring不建议使用</span></span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"><span class="cm-meta">@Service</span></span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"><span class="cm-keyword">public</span> <span class="cm-keyword">class</span> <span class="cm-def">UserService</span> {</span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"><span cm-text="" cm-zwsp="">
</span></span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"><span class="cm-comment">// &nbsp;  @Resource //表示根据类型进行注入</span></span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"> &nbsp; &nbsp;<span class="cm-meta">@Resource</span>(<span class="cm-variable">name</span> <span class="cm-operator">=</span> <span class="cm-string">"userDAOImpl1"</span>) <span class="cm-comment">//表示根据名称进行注入</span></span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"> &nbsp; &nbsp;<span class="cm-keyword">public</span> <span class="cm-variable">UserDAO</span> <span class="cm-variable">userDAO</span>;</span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"><span cm-text="" cm-zwsp="">
</span></span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"> &nbsp; &nbsp;<span class="cm-keyword">public</span> <span class="cm-variable-3">void</span> <span class="cm-variable">add</span>() {</span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"> &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;<span class="cm-variable">System</span>.<span class="cm-variable">out</span>.<span class="cm-variable">println</span>(<span class="cm-string">"Service add......."</span>);</span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"> &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;<span class="cm-variable">userDAO</span>.<span class="cm-variable">add</span>();</span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"> &nbsp;  }</span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;">}</span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"><span cm-text="" cm-zwsp="">
</span></span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"><span class="cm-comment">//@Value的使用</span></span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"><span class="cm-meta">@Value</span>(<span class="cm-variable">value</span> <span class="cm-operator">=</span> <span class="cm-string">"wjh"</span>)</span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"><span class="cm-keyword">private</span> <span class="cm-variable-3">String</span> <span class="cm-variable">name</span>;</span></pre></div></div></div></div></div><div style="position: absolute; height: 0px; width: 1px; border-bottom: 0px solid transparent; top: 845px;"></div><div class="CodeMirror-gutters" style="display: none; height: 845px;"></div></div></div></pre><h3 id='完全注解开发'><span>完全注解开发</span></h3><p><strong><span>使用配置类来代替xml的组件的扫描</span></strong></p><pre class="md-fences md-end-block ty-contain-cm modeLoaded" spellcheck="false" lang="java"><div class="CodeMirror cm-s-inner cm-s-null-scroll CodeMirror-wrap" lang="java"><div style="overflow: hidden; width: 1000px; height: 1em; outline: none;"></textarea></div><div class="CodeMirror-scrollbar-filler" cm-not-content="true"></div><div class="CodeMirror-gutter-filler" cm-not-content="true"></div><div class="CodeMirror-scroll" tabindex="-1"><div class="CodeMirror-sizer" style="margin-left: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; border-right-width: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px;"><div style="position: relative; top: 0px;"><div class="CodeMirror-lines" role="presentation"><div role="presentation" style="position: relative; outline: none;"><div class="CodeMirror-measure"><pre><span>xxxxxxxxxx</span></pre></div><div class="CodeMirror-measure"></div><div style="position: relative; z-index: 1;"></div><div class="CodeMirror-code" role="presentation" style=""><div class="CodeMirror-activeline" style="position: relative;"><div class="CodeMirror-activeline-background CodeMirror-linebackground"></div><div class="CodeMirror-gutter-background CodeMirror-activeline-gutter" style="left: 0px; width: 0px;"></div><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"><span class="cm-comment">//@Configuration 表示这个类是一个配置类</span></span></pre></div><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"><span class="cm-comment">//@ComponentScan 开启组件扫描</span></span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"><span class="cm-meta">@Configuration</span></span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"><span class="cm-meta">@ComponentScan</span>(<span class="cm-variable">basePackages</span> <span class="cm-operator">=</span> {<span class="cm-string">"com.wjh"</span>})</span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"><span class="cm-keyword">public</span> <span class="cm-keyword">class</span> <span class="cm-def">SpringConfig</span> {</span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;">}</span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"><span class="cm-variable">使用的时候需要把加载配置文件的方式改为加载配置类</span></span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"><span class="cm-variable">ApplicationContext</span> <span class="cm-variable">context</span> <span class="cm-operator">=</span> <span class="cm-keyword">new</span> <span class="cm-variable">AnnotationConfigApplicationContext</span>(<span class="cm-variable">SpringConfig</span>.<span class="cm-keyword">class</span>);</span></pre></div></div></div></div></div><div style="position: absolute; height: 0px; width: 1px; border-bottom: 0px solid transparent; top: 205px;"></div><div class="CodeMirror-gutters" style="display: none; height: 205px;"></div></div></div></pre><h2 id='aop概念）'><span>AOP（概念）</span></h2><p><strong><span>什么是AOP</span></strong></p><ul><li><span>面向切面编程，利用AOP可以对业务逻辑的各个部分进行分离，从而使得业务逻辑各个部分之间的耦合度降低，提高程序的可重用性，同时提高了开发效率</span></li><li><strong><span>简单的说就是：不修改源代码的情况下，在主干里面添加新功能</span></strong></li><li><strong><span>比如一个登录功能，如果想要添加一个权限验证的模块，传统方式需要修改源代码，但是使用AOP面向切面编程，可以不修改源代码就可以实现</span></strong></li></ul><h3 id='aop的底层原理'><span>AOP的底层原理</span></h3><ol start='' ><li><p><span>AOP底层使用动态代理</span></p><p><span>有两种情况动态代理</span></p><blockquote><p><span>第一种有接口的情况，</span><strong><span>使用JDK动态代理，创建接口的动态代理对象，增强类的方法</span></strong></p><p><span>第二种没有接口的情况，</span><strong><span>使用CGLIB动态代理，创建子类的代理对象，增强类的方法</span></strong></p></blockquote></li></ol><h3 id='aop-jdk动态代理是实现'><span>AOP-JDK动态代理是实现</span></h3><p><u><strong><span>在java.lang.reflect.Proxy中有一个newProxyInstance静态方法</span></strong></u></p><p><strong><span>里面有三个参数:</span></strong></p><ul><li><span>一个是当前类加载器</span></li><li><span>另一个是Class数组，里面放所要代理的接口interface</span></li><li><span>最后一个是InvocationHandler接口需要实现里面的invoke的方法，创建代理对象，写增强的方法</span></li></ul><p>&nbsp;</p><pre class="md-fences md-end-block ty-contain-cm modeLoaded" spellcheck="false" lang="java" style="break-inside: unset;"><div class="CodeMirror cm-s-inner cm-s-null-scroll CodeMirror-wrap" lang="java"><div style="overflow: hidden; position: relative; width: 3px; height: 0px; top: 10.8px; left: 4px;"><textarea autocorrect="off" autocapitalize="off" spellcheck="false" tabindex="0" style="position: absolute; bottom: -1em; padding: 0px; width: 1000px; height: 1em; outline: none;"></textarea></div><div class="CodeMirror-scrollbar-filler" cm-not-content="true"></div><div class="CodeMirror-gutter-filler" cm-not-content="true"></div><div class="CodeMirror-scroll" tabindex="-1"><div class="CodeMirror-sizer" style="margin-left: 0px; solid transparent; top: 1152px;"></div><div class="CodeMirror-gutters" style="display: none; height: 1152px;"></div></div></div></pre><h3 id='aop术语'><span>AOP术语</span></h3><ul><li><strong><span>连接点</span></strong></li></ul><blockquote><p><span>类里面的那些方法可以被增强，这些方法称为连接点</span></p></blockquote><ul><li><strong><span>切入点</span></strong></li></ul><blockquote><p><span>实际被增强的方法称为切入点</span></p></blockquote><ul><li><strong><span>通知（增强）</span></strong></li></ul><blockquote><p><span>实际增强的部分称为通知</span></p><p><span>通知有五种类型：</span></p><blockquote><p><span>前置通知</span></p><p><span>后置通知</span></p><p><span>环绕通知</span></p><p><span>异常通知</span></p><p><span>最终通知（finally）</span></p></blockquote></blockquote><ul><li><p><strong><span>切面</span></strong></p><p><span>把通知应用到切入点</span></p></li></ul><h3 id='aop的准备工作'><span>AOP的准备工作</span></h3><ol start='' ><li><span>Spring框架一般都是基于AspectJ实现AOP操作的</span></li><li><span>AspectJ不是Spring的组成部分，独立AOP框架，一般把Sprin和AspectJ框架一起使用来完成AOP操作</span></li><li><span>基于AspectJ实现AOP操作</span></li></ol><blockquote><p><span>基于xml配置</span></p><p><span>基于注解</span></p></blockquote><ol start='4' ><li><strong><span>在项目引入依赖</span></strong></li></ol><p><img src="Spring.assets/image-20220409235338414.png" referrerpolicy="no-referrer" alt="image-20220409235338414"></p><ol start='5' ><li><p><strong><span>切入点表达式</span></strong></p><p><span>切入点表达式的作用，知道对哪个类的那个方法进行增强</span></p><p><strong><span>语法结构:</span></strong></p><p><span>execution([权限修饰符] [返回类型] [类的全路径] [方法名]  ([参数列表]) )</span></p><p><span>举例一：excution(*com.wjh.dao.UserDAO.add(..)) //表示对com.wjh.dao.UserDAO类的add方法进行增强</span></p><p><span>举例二：excution(</span><em><span>com.wjh.dao.UserDAO.</span></em><span>(..)) //表示对com.wjh.dao.UserDAO类的所有方法进行增强</span></p><p><span>举例三：excution(</span><em><span>com.wjh.dao.</span></em><span>.*(..)) //表示对com.wjh.dao下的所有类的所有方法进行增强</span></p></li></ol><h3 id='aspectj注解使用'><span>AspectJ注解使用</span></h3><ol start='' ><li><p><span>先导入jar</span></p></li><li><p><span>创建一个user类和增强user的类userProxy</span></p></li><li><p><span>为user类和userProxy添加注解注入bean对象</span></p></li><li><p><span>开启注解扫描</span></p></li><li><p><span>开启AspectJ的生成代理对象可以使用xml，亦可以使用SpringConfig 完全注解模式</span></p><blockquote><pre class="md-fences md-end-block ty-contain-cm modeLoaded" spellcheck="false" lang="xml"><div class="CodeMirror cm-s-inner cm-s-null-scroll CodeMirror-wrap" lang="xml"><div style="overflow: hidden; position: relative; width: 3px; height: 0px; top: 10.8px; left: 4px;"><textarea autocorrect="off" autocapitalize="off" spellcheck="false" tabindex="0" style="position: absolute; bottom: -1em; padding: 0px; width: 1000px; height: 1em; outline: none;"></textarea></div><div class="CodeMirror-scrollbar-filler" cm-not-content="true"></div><div class="CodeMirror-gutter-filler" cm-not-content="true"></div><div class="CodeMirror-scroll" tabindex="-1"><div class="CodeMirror-sizer" style="margin-left: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; border-right-width: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px;"><div style="position: relative; top: 0px;"><div class="CodeMirror-lines" role="presentation"><div role="presentation" style="position: relative; outline: none;"><div class="CodeMirror-measure"><pre><span>xxxxxxxxxx</span></pre></div><div class="CodeMirror-measure"></div><div style="position: relative; z-index: 1;"></div><div class="CodeMirror-code" role="presentation" style=""><div class="CodeMirror-activeline" style="position: relative;"><div class="CodeMirror-activeline-background CodeMirror-linebackground"></div><div class="CodeMirror-gutter-background CodeMirror-activeline-gutter" style="left: 0px; width: 0px;"></div><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;">xml:</span></pre></div><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"><span class="cm-comment">&lt;!--开启注解扫描--&gt;</span></span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"><span class="cm-tag cm-bracket">&lt;</span><span class="cm-tag">context:component-scan</span> <span class="cm-attribute">base-package</span>=<span class="cm-string">"com.wjh.learnspring3.aopannotation"</span><span class="cm-tag cm-bracket">&gt;&lt;/</span><span class="cm-tag">context:component-scan</span><span class="cm-tag cm-bracket">&gt;</span></span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"><span class="cm-comment">&lt;!--开启AspectJ生成代理对象--&gt;</span></span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"><span class="cm-tag cm-bracket">&lt;</span><span class="cm-tag">aop:aspectj-autoproxy</span><span class="cm-tag cm-bracket">&gt;&lt;/</span><span class="cm-tag">aop:aspectj-autoproxy</span><span class="cm-tag cm-bracket">&gt;</span></span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"><span cm-text="" cm-zwsp="">
</span></span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;">java:</span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;">@Configuration</span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;">@ComponentScan(basePackages = {"com.wjh.learnspring3.aopannotation"}) //开启组件扫描</span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;">@EnableAspectJAutoProxy //开启AspectJ生成代理对象</span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;">public class SpringConfig {</span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;">}</span></pre></div></div></div></div></div><div style="position: absolute; height: 0px; width: 1px; border-bottom: 0px solid transparent; top: 307px;"></div><div class="CodeMirror-gutters" style="display: none; height: 307px;"></div></div></div></pre></blockquote></li><li><p><span>在userProxy类中加入注解@Aspect生成代理对象,以及五种通知的使用</span></p><blockquote><pre class="md-fences md-end-block ty-contain-cm modeLoaded" spellcheck="false" lang="java" style="break-inside: unset;"><div class="CodeMirror cm-s-inner cm-s-null-scroll CodeMirror-wrap" lang="java"><div style="overflow: hidden; height: 512px;"></div></div></div></pre><ol start='2' ><li><p><span>创建一个dao和service，并在service引入dao属性,在dao中引入JdbcTemplate属性，使用注解进行对象创建</span></p><pre class="md-fences md-end-block ty-contain-cm modeLoaded" spellcheck="false" lang="java" style="break-inside: unset;"><div class="CodeMirror cm-s-inner cm-s-null-scroll CodeMirror-wrap" lang="java"><div style="overflow: hidden; </span></span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"> &nbsp; &nbsp;<span class="cm-comment">/*删除操作*/</span></span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"> &nbsp; &nbsp;<span class="cm-meta">@Override</span></span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"> &nbsp; &nbsp;<span class="cm-keyword">public</span> <span class="cm-variable-3">void</span> <span class="cm-variable">deleteNote</span>(<span class="cm-variable-3">Integer</span> <span class="cm-variable">noteId</span>) {</span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"> &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;<span class="cm-variable">jdbcTemplate</span>.<span class="cm-variable">update</span>(<span class="cm-string">"delete from t_note where id = ?"</span>, <span class="cm-variable">noteId</span>);</span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"><span cm-text="" cm-zwsp="">
</span></span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"> &nbsp;  }</span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"><span cm-text="" cm-zwsp="">
</span></span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"> &nbsp; &nbsp;<span class="cm-comment">/*获取行数特殊值的操作，使用queryForObject(String sql,Class[] class)</span></span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"> &nbsp; &nbsp; <span class="cm-comment">* sql:指的是执行的sql</span></span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"> &nbsp; &nbsp; <span class="cm-comment">* class 指的是返回的基本数据类型</span></span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"> &nbsp; &nbsp; <span class="cm-comment">* */</span></span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"> &nbsp; &nbsp;<span class="cm-meta">@Override</span></span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"> &nbsp; &nbsp;<span class="cm-keyword">public</span> <span class="cm-variable-3">int</span> <span class="cm-variable">NoteCount</span>() {</span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"> &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;<span class="cm-variable-3">Integer</span> <span class="cm-variable">count</span> <span class="cm-operator">=</span> <span class="cm-variable">jdbcTemplate</span>.<span class="cm-variable">queryForObject</span>(<span class="cm-string">"select count(*) from t_note"</span>, <span class="cm-variable-3">Integer</span>.<span class="cm-keyword">class</span>);</span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"> &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;<span class="cm-keyword">return</span> <span class="cm-variable">count</span>;</span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"> &nbsp;  }</span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"><span cm-text="" cm-zwsp="">
</span></span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"> &nbsp; &nbsp;<span class="cm-comment">/*查询返回自定义类型</span></span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"> &nbsp; &nbsp; <span class="cm-comment">* queryForObject(String sql, RowMapper&lt;T&gt; rowMapper ,Object...args)</span></span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"> &nbsp; &nbsp; <span class="cm-comment">* RowMapper&lt;T&gt; 是一个接口，返回一个自定义类型的类需要实现接口中的BeanPropertyRowMapper&lt;T&gt;(T.class)方法</span></span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"> &nbsp; &nbsp; <span class="cm-comment">* BeanPropertyRowMapper&lt;T&gt;(T.class) 这个T 是返回的类型 ， T.class 是返回的类型的class</span></span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"> &nbsp; &nbsp; <span class="cm-comment">* */</span></span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"> &nbsp; &nbsp;<span class="cm-meta">@Override</span></span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"> &nbsp; &nbsp;<span class="cm-keyword">public</span> <span class="cm-variable">Note</span> <span class="cm-variable">getNoteById</span>(<span class="cm-variable-3">Integer</span> <span class="cm-variable">id</span>) {</span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"> &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;<span class="cm-keyword">return</span> <span class="cm-variable">jdbcTemplate</span>.<span class="cm-variable">queryForObject</span>(<span class="cm-string">"select * from t_note where id = ?"</span>, <span class="cm-keyword">new</span> <span class="cm-variable">BeanPropertyRowMapper</span><span class="cm-operator">&lt;</span><span class="cm-variable">Note</span><span class="cm-operator">&gt;</span>(<span class="cm-variable">Note</span>.<span class="cm-keyword">class</span>), <span class="cm-variable">id</span>);</span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"> &nbsp;  }</span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"><span cm-text="" cm-zwsp="">
</span></span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"> &nbsp; &nbsp;<span class="cm-comment">/*查询返回集合</span></span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"> &nbsp; &nbsp; <span class="cm-comment">* query(String sql ,RowMapper&lt;T&gt; rowMapper )</span></span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"> &nbsp; width: 1px; border-bottom: 0px solid transparent; top: 2970px;"></div><div class="CodeMirror-gutters" style="display: none; height: 2970px;"></div></div></div></pre><h2 id='事务'><span>事务</span></h2><h3 id='事务概念'><span>事务概念</span></h3><ol start='' ><li><p><strong><span>什么是事务？</span></strong></p><p><span>事务是数据库操作的基本单元，逻辑上一组操作，要么都成功，如果有一个失败全部都会失败</span></p></li><li><p><strong><span>事务的四个特性（ACID性）</span></strong></p><blockquote><p><strong><span>原子性：</span></strong><span> 表示事务是一个不可分割，要么都成功要么都失败</span></p><p><strong><span>一致性：</span></strong><span> 操作之前和操作之后总量不变</span></p><p><strong><span>隔离性：</span></strong><span> 操作同一个数据库每个事务之间不影响</span></p><p><strong><span>持久性：</span></strong><span> 数据的持久性</span></p></blockquote></li></ol><h3 id='spring中的事务管理'><span>Spring中的事务管理</span></h3><ol start='' ><li><p><span>事务添加是在JaveEE三层结构上的service层</span></p></li><li><p><span>在Spring中进行事务管理</span></p><p><span>有两种方式: 编程式和声明式(开发中使用这个)</span></p></li><li><p><span>声明式事务管理</span></p><ol start='' ><li><span>基于xml</span></li><li><span>基于注解</span></li></ol></li><li><p><span>Spring中的事务管理底层使用的是AOP的概念</span></p></li><li><p><span>Spring事务管理的API</span></p><ul><li><span>PlatformTransactionManager 接口代表事务管理器,这个接口针对不同的框架有不同的实现类</span></li><li><span>针对jdbcTemplate使用的是DataSourceTransactionManager</span></li><li><span>针对Mabitas使用的也是DataSourceTransactionManager</span></li><li><span>针对Hibernate使用的是HibernateTransactionManager</span></li></ul></li></ol><h3 id='spring声明式事务注解方式'><span>Spring声明式事务(注解方式)</span></h3><h4 id='注解方式的开启步骤'><strong><span>注解方式的开启步骤</span></strong><span>:</span></h4><ul><li><p><span>创建事务管理器</span></p><pre class="md-fences md-end-block ty-contain-cm modeLoaded" spellcheck="false" lang="xml"><div class="CodeMirror cm-s-inner cm-s-null-scroll CodeMirror-wrap" lang="xml"><div style="overflow: hidden; outline: none;"><div class="CodeMirror-measure"><pre><span>xxxxxxxxxx</span></pre></div><div class="CodeMirror-measure"></div><div style="position: relative; z-index: 1;"></div><div class="CodeMirror-code" role="presentation"><div class="CodeMirror-activeline" style="position: relative;"><div class="CodeMirror-activeline-background CodeMirror-linebackground"></div><div class="CodeMirror-gutter-background CodeMirror-activeline-gutter" style="left: 0px; width: 0px;"></div><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"><span class="cm-meta">@Service</span></span></pre></div><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"><span class="cm-meta">@Transactional</span> <span class="cm-comment">//开启事务</span></span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"><span class="cm-keyword">public</span> <span class="cm-keyword">class</span> <span class="cm-def">MoneyService</span> {</span></pre></div></div></div></div></div><div style="position: absolute; height: 0px; width: 1px; border-bottom: 0px solid transparent; top: 77px;"></div><div class="CodeMirror-gutters" style="display: none; height: 77px;"></div></div></div></pre><p><strong><span>在@Transactional中有六个参数</span></strong></p><ul><li><p><strong><span>propagation -事务传播行为</span></strong></p><ul><li><span>REQUIRED : 多事务方法直接调用,如果该方法有事务,调用另一个方法时,如果另一个方法没有事务则会使用该方法的事务   (默认) , 如果a方法和b方法都没有事务,表示创建一个新的事务</span></li><li><span>REQUIRED _NEW :调用另一个方法的时候,会自动创建一个新的事务</span></li></ul></li><li><p><strong><span>isolation -事务隔离级别</span></strong></p><p><span>事务有隔离级别,多个事务之间不影响,</span></p><p><span>有三个读问题: 脏读,不可重复读,幻读</span></p><p><strong><span>脏读:</span></strong><span>一个未提交的事务,读取到另一个未提交的数据</span></p><p><strong><span>不可重复读</span></strong><span>:一个未提交的事务,读取另一个已经提交的数据</span></p><p><strong><span>幻读:</span></strong><span>一个未提交的事务,读取到一个添加的数据</span></p><ul><li><span>默认是REPEATABLE_READ ,可重复读</span></li><li><span>SERIALIZABLE 串行化,可以解决三种读问题</span></li></ul></li><li><p><strong><span>timeout:超时时间</span></strong></p><p><span>事务在一定时间内必须提交,不提交的话会回滚数据 ,默认是-1表示不超时</span></p></li><li><p><strong><span>readOnly: 是否只读</span></strong></p><p><span>读: 查询数据  </span><span>	</span><span>写: 增删改</span></p><p><span>默认是readOnly是false 表示可读可写 未true的话表示只能读</span></p></li><li><p><strong><span>rollBackFor:回滚</span></strong><span> </span></p><p><span>出现什么异常进行回滚</span></p></li><li><p><strong><span>noRollBackFor:回滚</span></strong></p><p><span>出现什么异常不进行回滚</span></p></li></ul><h3 id='spring声明式事务基于xml'><span>Spring声明式事务(基于xml)</span></h3><p><strong><span>步骤</span></strong></p><ol start='' ><li><p><span>配置事务管理器</span></p><pre class="md-fences md-end-block ty-contain-cm modeLoaded" spellcheck="false" lang="xml" style="break-inside: unset;"><div class="CodeMirror cm-s-inner cm-s-null-scroll CodeMirror-wrap" lang="xml"><div style="overflow: hidden; position: relative; width: 3px; height: 0px; top: 10.8px; left: 4px;"><textarea autocorrect="off" autocapitalize="off" spellcheck="false" tabindex="0" style="position: absolute; bottom: -1em; padding: 0px; </span></span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"> &nbsp; &nbsp;<span class="cm-comment">&lt;!--开启组件扫描--&gt;</span></span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"> &nbsp; &nbsp;<span class="cm-tag cm-bracket">&lt;</span><span class="cm-tag">context:component-scan</span> <span class="cm-attribute">base-package</span>=<span class="cm-string">"com.wjh"</span><span class="cm-tag cm-bracket">/&gt;</span></span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"> &nbsp; &nbsp;<span class="cm-comment">&lt;!--加载数据库配置文件--&gt;</span></span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"> &nbsp; &nbsp;<span class="cm-tag cm-bracket">&lt;</span><span class="cm-tag">context:property-placeholder</span> <span class="cm-attribute">location</span>=<span class="cm-string">"classpath:jdbc.properties"</span><span class="cm-tag cm-bracket">/&gt;</span></span></pre><pre class=" CodeMirror-line " role="presentation"><span role="presentation" style="padding-right: 0.1px;"> &nbsp;
